NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING 
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES 
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER 
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Commissioner  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
	
S. Vinothkumar a male child, son of Thiru Subramanian, born on 10th September 2001, residing at No. 1/199, 
Rajeev Gandhi Nagar, Ulaganeri, Madurai-625 107, has been living as  Transgender Woman. I have been granted Identity 
Card No. MDU/051/2021, issued by Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board, Social Welfare and NMP Department. 
By this, I may be treated as aTransgender woman and shall henceforth be known  as S. YOGASRI.
Madurai,	
S. VINOTHKUMAR
22nd December 2021.
	
M. Nagappan a male child, son of Thiru M. Manickam, born on 30th May 1992, residing at No. 224/103, 
5th Street, Sasthri Nagar, Chennai-600 084, has been living as Transgender Woman. I have been granted Identity 
Card No. CHN/116/2019, issued by Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board, Social Welfare and NMP Department. 
By this, I may be treated as a  Transgender Woman and shall henceforth be known  as ARUNA MANICKAM.
Chennai,	
M. NAGAPPAN
22nd December 2021.
	
R. Rajesh a male child, son of Thiru R. Ramesh,  born on 14th August 1994, residing at No.  138/5, Vanniyar Street, 
Kodambakkam, Chennai-600 024, has been living as a Trans Women. I have been granted Identity Card No. CHN/568/2021, 
issued by Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board, Social Welfare and NMP Department. By this, I may be treated 
as a Trans Women and shall henceforth be known  as R. RESHMA.
Chennai,	
R. RAJESH
23rd December 2021.
